\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}
Lock-\/free skip-\/list set (template specialization for \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_desc}{RCU}) 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu}%
 The implementation of well-\/known probabilistic data structure called skip-\/list invented by W.\+Pugh in his papers\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}1989\mbox{]} W.\+Pugh Skip Lists\+: \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} Probabilistic Alternative to Balanced Trees
\item \mbox{[}1990\mbox{]} W.\+Pugh \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} Skip \doxylink{class_list}{List} Cookbook
\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} skip-\/list is a probabilistic data structure that provides expected logarithmic time search without the need of rebalance. The skip-\/list is a collection of sorted linked list. Nodes are ordered by key. Each node is linked into a subset of the lists. Each list has a level, ranging from 0 to 32. The bottom-\/level list contains all the nodes, and each higher-\/level list is a sublist of the lower-\/level lists. Each node is created with a random top level (with a random height), and belongs to all lists up to that level. The probability that a node has the height 1 is 1/2. The probability that a node has the height N is 1/2 \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} N (more precisely, the distribution depends on an random generator provided, but our generators have this property).

The lock-\/free variant of skip-\/list is implemented according to book
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}2008\mbox{]} M.\+Herlihy, N.\+Shavit "{}\+The Art of Multiprocessor Programming"{}, chapter 14.\+4 "{}\+A Lock-\/\+Free Concurrent Skiplist"{}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\bfseries{Template arguments}}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ type to be stored in the list. The type must be based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1node}{skip\+\_\+list\+::node}} (for {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1base__hook}{skip\+\_\+list\+::base\+\_\+hook}}) or it must have a member of type {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1node}{skip\+\_\+list\+::node}} (for {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1member__hook}{skip\+\_\+list\+::member\+\_\+hook}}).
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ set traits, default is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1traits}{skip\+\_\+list\+::traits}} It is possible to declare option-\/based list with {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1make__traits}{cds\+::intrusive\+::skip\+\_\+list\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction instead of {\ttfamily Traits} template argument.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{skip__list__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/skip\+\_\+list\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files.
\end{DoxyNote}
{\bfseries{Iterators}}

The class supports a forward iterator (\doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_abb44322abdc57c532066f52995fd623a}{iterator} and \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aaf1247e2dec27d2973dff9e91d70c2d3}{const\+\_\+iterator}). The iteration is ordered.

You may iterate over skip-\/list set items only under RCU lock. Only in this case the iterator is thread-\/safe since while RCU is locked any set\textquotesingle{}s item cannot be reclaimed.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The requirement of RCU lock during iterating means that any type of modification of the skip list (i.\+e. inserting, erasing and so on) is not possible.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The iterator object cannot be passed between threads.
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\bfseries{How to use}}

You should incorporate \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1node}{skip\+\_\+list\+::node} into your struct {\ttfamily T} and provide appropriate \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1traits_aeabd2876dac1fa7dddb475b175728dfa}{skip\+\_\+list\+::traits\+::hook} in your {\ttfamily Traits} template parameters. Usually, for {\ttfamily Traits} you define a struct based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1skip__list_1_1traits}{skip\+\_\+list\+::traits}}.

Example for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1general__buffered}{cds\+::urcu\+::general\+\_\+buffered$<$$>$}} RCU and base hook\+:

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Include\ RCU\ skip-\/list\ specialization}}

Iterator type 

The forward iterator has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item to protect the value, the iterator contains a GC-\/specific guard + another guard is required locally for increment operator. For some GC (like as {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1gc_af0523881f089593a7559d194ee2b5dd9}{gc\+::\+HP}}), a guard is a limited resource per thread, so an exception (or assertion) "{}no free guard"{} may be thrown if the limit of guard count per thread is exceeded.
\item The iterator cannot be moved across thread boundary because it contains thread-\/private GC\textquotesingle{}s guard.
\item Iterator ensures thread-\/safety even if you delete the item the iterator points to. However, in case of concurrent deleting operations there is no guarantee that you iterate all item in the list. Moreover, a crash is possible when you try to iterate the next element that has been deleted by concurrent thread.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Use this iterator on the concurrent container for debugging purpose only.
\end{DoxyWarning}

typedef skip\+\_\+list\+::details\+::iterator$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae2e96fd2856b64d703d2a34ac96bd360}{gc}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aee3cb013f99cb4859f7e596f21abdaac}{node\+\_\+traits}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a6718bca72647b89ba51bb2c2abefd3a5}{back\+\_\+off}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::iterator}



Forward iterator 

The forward iterator has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item it depends on iterator of underlying {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

You may safely use iterators in multi-\/threaded environment only under RCU lock. Otherwise, a crash is possible if another thread deletes the element the iterator points to. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a849c671dc85572a1c40a83bdbbb6aac5}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!key\_comparator@{key\_comparator}}

Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} 

The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns {\ttfamily true} if it is found, and {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::contains (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is similar to {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad8ec23e567f2b257271d463c79e74cc1}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

Deletes the item from the set 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_erase}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_erase}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns {\ttfamily true}. If the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

Note the hash functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a442cc388b70130898a6a40e53e5286b6}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}

Deletes the item from the set 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_erase}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_erase}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns {\ttfamily true}. If the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a1831116fe2eaea39643d3fcb65371d5b}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the set 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_erase_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_erase_func}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, call {\ttfamily f} functor with item found, unlinks it from the set, and returns {\ttfamily true}. The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3c7121095d7eac4eb4b933d8cb1593c2}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously.

The {\ttfamily Func} interface is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{value\_type}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


If the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ad32a11bac9ebb7da30d01c46637dc7}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}
\index{erase@{erase}!cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase()}{erase()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ad32a11bac9ebb7da30d01c46637dc7}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the set 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_erase_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_erase_func}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, call {\ttfamily f} functor with item found, unlinks it from the set, and returns {\ttfamily true}. The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3c7121095d7eac4eb4b933d8cb1593c2}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously.

The {\ttfamily Func} interface is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{value\_type}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 If the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

Note the hash functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked. 函数调用图\+:

Delete the item from the set with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_erase}{erase(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_ad7e1caa5f872abb2fd071c6b6d43f016}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

Deletes the item from the set with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_erase}{erase(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a06b7ec55a6a3f0005cbf03a3829a67c7}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a212bbe201e4230e902ec3ec41c345a79}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a90b615614b9ee394bd38a60d71bb4156} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the set with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns it as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The {\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} specified in class\textquotesingle{} template parameters when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_acec5e2a6e4d638922062599b9bc2c972} 
template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154916824e4486e601d733e5dea6419a}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the set with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item found. If the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154916824e4486e601d733e5dea6419a}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked. The function does not call the disposer for the item found. The disposer will be implicitly invoked when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. Example\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a5e17af7064fa115bb4ef40789beac714} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+max (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with maximal key from the list 

The function searches an item with maximal key, unlinks it, and returns the pointer to item as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Due the concurrent nature of the list, the function extracts {\itshape nearly} maximal key. It means that the function gets rightmost item and tries to unlink it. During unlinking, a concurrent thread may insert an item with key greater than rightmost item\textquotesingle{}s key. So, the function returns the item with maximum key at the moment of list traversing.
\end{DoxyNote}
The {\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously when returned \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+min (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with minimal key from the list 

The function searches an item with minimal key, unlinks it, and returns it as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Due the concurrent nature of the list, the function extracts {\itshape nearly} minimum key. It means that the function gets leftmost item and tries to unlink it. During unlinking, a concurrent thread may insert an item with key less than leftmost item\textquotesingle{}s key. So, the function returns the item with minimum key at the moment of list traversing.
\end{DoxyNote}
The {\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} automatically when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the set with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_extract}{extract(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a89b1011b91ab75523d467c4b6abb96f8}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}
\index{extract\_with@{extract\_with}!cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a154916824e4486e601d733e5dea6419a}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the set with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_acec5e2a6e4d638922062599b9bc2c972}{extract(\+Q const\&)}} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a3dc70165841bf8871caed0a1f8c0dece}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}

Finds {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_find_func}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor can change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the set {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

Note the compare functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab45b22396c7702dbac0f1f9fc806cf7f}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}
\index{find@{find}!cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{find()}{find()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab45b22396c7702dbac0f1f9fc806cf7f} 
template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_find_func}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor can change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the set {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

The {\ttfamily key} argument is non-\/const since it can be used as {\ttfamily f} functor destination i.\+e., the functor can modify both arguments.

The function applies RCU lock internally.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. 函数调用图\+:

Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the pointer to the item found as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empt guarded pointer.

The {\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously when returned \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a758da15b68e18ac7bd73c0f4aeae67f8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns a {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aee29a4d37f751c9435af273ebc775f5b}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} object pointed to item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found it returns empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aee29a4d37f751c9435af273ebc775f5b}{raw\+\_\+ptr}}.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU should be locked before call of this function. Returned item is valid only while RCU is locked\+:

Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_hp_get}{get( Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a26c8bc07223704372b899ff5d41c5144}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!get\_with@{get\_with}}

Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_SkipListSet_rcu_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

Inserts new node 

The function inserts {\ttfamily val} in the set if it does not contain an item with key equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Inserts new node 

The function inserts {\ttfamily val} in the set if it does not contain an item with key equal to {\ttfamily val}.

The function applies RCU lock internally.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is placed into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a8cce1422756e1f63a84f67c5a78d9553}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this set\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a7e449602a3c25565f0e76ac59b172b49}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}

Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this set\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked. 函数调用图\+:

size\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ac42c05b5701aef6bab82675cf3b55fee}{\+::size}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Returns item count in the set 

The value returned depends on item counter type provided by {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter. If it is {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1atomicity_1_1empty__item__counter}{atomicity\+::empty\+\_\+item\+\_\+counter}} this function always returns 0. Therefore, the function is not suitable for checking the set emptiness, use {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a99eb9c3f838b406d476f5bec77f82e91}{empty()}} for this purpose. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0ad0e95249f8442e4b28accd24d9479b}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!size@{size}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unlink()}{unlink()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a6c0561887682f47f5358170b6a87ca18} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::unlink (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the set 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the set and unlink it from the set if it is found and is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Difference between {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a748d299ed5f62bd994b6abe64a38d7b8}{erase()}} and {\ttfamily unlink}() functions\+: {\ttfamily erase}() finds {\itshape a key} and deletes the item found. {\ttfamily unlink}() finds an item by key and deletes it only if {\ttfamily val} is an item of that set, i.\+e. the pointer to item found is equal to {\ttfamily  \&val }.

The {\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a147b2eb75b2c1a083f61f50e42d35384}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!unlink@{unlink}}
\index{unlink@{unlink}!cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unlink()}{unlink()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a147b2eb75b2c1a083f61f50e42d35384} 
template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::unlink (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the set 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the set and unlink it from the set if it is found and is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Difference between {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a748d299ed5f62bd994b6abe64a38d7b8}{erase()}} and {\ttfamily unlink}() functions\+: {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a748d299ed5f62bd994b6abe64a38d7b8}{erase()}} finds {\itshape a key} and deletes the item found. {\ttfamily unlink}() searches an item by key and deletes it only if {\ttfamily val} is an item of that set, i.\+e. the pointer to item found is equal to {\ttfamily  \&val }.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3c7121095d7eac4eb4b933d8cb1593c2}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a0e6e350a7f0f6128e429b6a54668e0d2}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!update@{update}}
\index{update@{update}!cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_a0e6e350a7f0f6128e429b6a54668e0d2} 
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the node 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} is not found in the set, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor {\ttfamily func} signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the set
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refer to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Returns std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, i.\+e. the node has been inserted or updated, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already exists.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting} 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aabb264b540f724ea27ba41db3199946f}\index{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!update@{update}}
\index{update@{update}!cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::SkipListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aabb264b540f724ea27ba41db3199946f} 
template$<$class RCU, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename Func$>$ \\
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Skip\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the node 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} is not found in the set, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87eb39e183716059cc1c726a7052bae9}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_skip_list_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the set
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refer to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor can change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

Returns std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, i.\+e. the node has been inserted or updated, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already exists.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting} 
\end{DoxyWarning}
